class="result-card__contents profile-result-card__contents"><h3 class="result-card__title profile-result-card__title">Ana Martín Rivillo</h3><h4 class="result-card__subtitle profile-result-card__subtitle">Artificial [In]telligence Recruiter @ LinkedIn</h4><div class="result-card__meta profile-result-card__meta"><p class="profile-result-card__location"></p></div></div></li><div class="description__text description__text--rich">LinkedIn’s Analytics team leverages big data to empower business decisions and deliver data-driven insights, metrics, and tools in order to drive member engagement, business growth, and monetization efforts.<br><br>We are now seeking a Data Scientist for a unique opportunity directly supporting global leadership. This person will work closely with various cross-functional teams such as product, marketing, sales, engineering, finance, and operations to develop and deliver metrics, analyses, solutions, and insights, with actionable recommendations for our international strategy. You will have the opportunity to work with some of the best data people anywhere in an environment which truly values (read: is obsessed with) data-driven decisions. Your sand-box will be a dataset representing an economic graph of the world. Successful candidates will have a passion for data exploration, automation, and plain old ‘getting stuff done’.<br><br>Responsibilities<br>● Analyze and mash-up massive amounts of data to mine useful business insights;<br>● Design and develop core business metrics, create insightful automated dashboards and data visualizations to track them and extract useful business insights;<br>● Work with different business and technical teams across the company to establish unified definitions, systems, and data governance for key metrics.<br>● Build scalable backend solutions for automation of data processing;<br>● Develop predictive/segmentation models to understand member behavior and impact on LinkedIn product/marketing/sales;<br>● Initiate and drive projects to completion with minimal guidance<br>● Communicate findings to internal teams and evangelize data-driven business decisions<br><br>Basic Qualifications<br>● Masters or PhD degree in a quantitative or hard science discipline: statistics, operations research, computer science, informatics, engineering, applied mathematics, economics, physics, chemistry<br>● 3+ years of industry experience in technical role, or in relevant industry (e-commerce, social network, job site, large sales operation)<br>● Programming skills with Python, R, Java, or equivalent language.<br>● Programming skills with SQL (psql/mysql/presto/hive/etc)<br>● Experience with ETL (moving data between systems)<br>● Experience with some data visualization tool (eg. Tableau, BI dashboarding, JS charting libraries,, R visualization packages, Python visualization libraries, etc.)<br><br>Preferred Qualifications<br>● Experience in Hadoop or other MapReduce paradigms and associated languages such as Pig and Hive;<br>● Experience with code repository/versioning system (git/svn/etc)<br>● Experience with Unix/Linux environment for automating processes with shell scripting.<br>● Experience with manipulating massive-scale structured and unstructured data;<br>● Understanding of different data stores, query tuning for different databases; performance tuning<br>● Experience in marketing and sales, being an innovator and disruptor is also a plus;<br>Being self-motivated, creative and collaborative;<br>● Excellent communications skills, with the ability to synthesize, simplify and explain complex problems to different types of audience, including executives<br><br><br><br>Global Data Privacy Notice for Job Candidates<br>This document provides transparency around the way in which LinkedIn handles personal data of employees and job applicants: https://lnkd.in/GlobalDataPrivacyNotice<br><br>All Dublin jobs at LinkedIn are available under our ReturnIn Scheme, for people returning to work from family or care responsibilities. This will include extra support through interview stage, and if successful, an extended induction according to your needs. To access the scheme just let your recruiter know that you're a returner when you apply.</div><ul class="job-criteria__list"><li class="job-criteria__item"><h3 class="job-criteria__subheader">Seniority level</h3><span class="job-criteria__text job-criteria__text--criteria">Not Applicable</span></li><li class="job-criteria__item"><h3 class="job-criteria__subheader">Employment type</h3><span class="job-criteria__text job-criteria__text--criteria">Full-time</span></li><li class="job-criteria__item"><h3 class="job-criteria__subheader">Job function</h3><span class="job-criteria__text job-criteria__text--criteria">Analyst</span></li><li class="job-criteria__item"><h3 class="job-criteria__subheader">Industries</h3><span class="job-criteria__text job-criteria__text--criteria">Internet</span><span class="job-criteria__text job-criteria__text--criteria">Information Technology and Services</span></li></ul></section><code style="display: none;" id="wwwEasyApplyUrl"><!--"https://www.linkedin.com/jobs/view/1605314842?showGuestApplyModal=true"--></code><code style="display: none;" id="decoratedJobPostingId"><!--"1605314842"--></code><code style="display: none;" id="searchId"><!--"04d4f7d4-fe07-4a42-83f4-d20fdc52f520"--></code></div></section></main><section class="related-jserps"><section class="expandable-link-columns"><div class="show-more-less"><button class="show-more-less__more-button show-more-less__button" aria-expanded="false" data-tracking-control-name="guest_job_search_show_more">More searches<li-icon class="show-more-less__button--chevron lazy-loaded" aria-hidden="true"><svg id="chevron-up-icon" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16px" height="16px" preserveAspectRatio="xMinYMin meet" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" version="1.1" focusable="false" class="show-more-less__button--chevron lazy-loaded">
